   7: def get_label_from_ID(length, y_allowed, ID):
   8:     parsed = ID.replace('ant_data__', '')
   9: 
  10:     index_value = 1
  11:     
  12:     if y_allowed:
  13:         index_value = 2
  14: 
  15:     states = np.empty((length, index_value), dtype=float)
  16: 
  17:     for i in range(length):
  18:         vec_string = re.sub(r'__.*', '', parsed)
  19: 
  20:         first = re.sub(r'_.*', '', vec_string)
  21: 
  22:         if y_allowed:
  23:             states[i][0] = int(first)
  24: 
  25:         first += '_'
  26:         second = re.sub(first, '', vec_string)

  28:             states[i][1] = int(second)
  29:         else:
  30:             states[i][0] = int(second)
  31:

  34:             remove_vec = vec_string + "__"
  35:             parsed = re.sub(remove_vec, '', parsed)
  36: 
  37:     return np.squeeze(states)

   1: def keras_fmin_fnct(space):

   5: 
   6:     def not_quite_linear(x):
   7:         return K.tanh(x / 5.0) * 5.0
   8: 
   9:     def linear_bound_above_abs_1(x):
  10:         return K.switch(K.less(not_quite_linear(x), 0), x - 1, x + 1)
  11:     
  12:     get_custom_objects().update({'linear_bound_above_abs_1': Activation(linear_bound_above_abs_1)})
  13:     get_custom_objects().update({'not_quite_linear': Activation(not_quite_linear)})
  14:     #model = Sequential()

  16:     kernel_size_0 = space['kernel_size_0']

  18:     
  19:     def resnet_layer(inputs,
  20:                     num_filters=16,
  21:                     kernel_size=3,
  22:                     strides=1,
  23:                     activation='relu',
  24:                     batch_normalization=True,
  25:                     conv_first=True):
  26:         """2D Convolution-Batch Normalization-Activation stack builder
  27:     
  28:         # Arguments
  29:             inputs (tensor): input tensor from input image or previous layer
  30:             num_filters (int): Convolution2D number of filters
  31:             kernel_size (int): Convolution2D square kernel dimensions
  32:             strides (int): Convolution2D square stride dimensions
  33:             activation (string): activation name
  34:             batch_normalization (bool): whether to include batch normalization
  35:             conv_first (bool): conv-bn-activation (True) or
  36:                 bn-activation-conv (False)
  37:     
  38:         # Returns
  39:             x (tensor): tensor as input to the next layer
  40:         """
  41:         conv = Convolution2D(num_filters,
  42:                       kernel_size=kernel_size,
  43:                       strides=strides,
  44:                       padding='valid',
  45:                       kernel_initializer='he_normal',
  46:                       kernel_regularizer=l2(1e-4))
  47:     
  48:         x = inputs
  49:         
  50:         if kernel_size != 1:
  51:             x  = torus_transform_layer((kernel_size, kernel_size))(x)
  52:         
  53:         if conv_first:
  54:             x = conv(x)
  55:             if batch_normalization:
  56:                 x = BatchNormalization()(x)
  57:             if activation is not None:
  58:                 x = Activation(activation)(x)
  59:         else:
  60:             if batch_normalization:
  61:                 x = BatchNormalization()(x)
  62:             if activation is not None:
  63:                 x = Activation(activation)(x)
  64:             x = conv(x)
  65:         return x
  66: 
  67:     def resnet_v2(input_shape, depth, num_classes):
  68:         """ResNet Version 2 Model builder [b]
  69:     
  70:         Stacks of (1 x 1)-(3 x 3)-(1 x 1) BN-ReLU-Convolution2D or also known as
  71:         bottleneck layer
  72:         First shortcut connection per layer is 1 x 1 Convolution2D.
  73:         Second and onwards shortcut connection is identity.
  74:         At the beginning of each stage, the feature map size is halved (downsampled)
  75:         by a convolutional layer with strides=2, while the number of filter maps is
  76:         doubled. Within each stage, the layers have the same number filters and the
  77:         same filter map sizes.
  78:         Features maps sizes:
  79:         conv1  : 32x32,  16
  80:         stage 0: 32x32,  64
  81:         stage 1: 16x16, 128
  82:         stage 2:  8x8,  256
  83:     
  84:         # Arguments
  85:             input_shape (tensor): shape of input image tensor
  86:             depth (int): number of core convolutional layers
  87:             num_classes (int): number of classes (CIFAR10 has 10)
  88:     
  89:         # Returns
  90:             model (Model): Keras model instance
  91:         """
  92:         if (depth - 2) % 9 != 0:
  93:             raise ValueError('depth should be 9n+2 (eg 56 or 110 in [b])')
  94:         # Start model definition.
  95:         num_filters_in = 16
  96:         num_res_blocks = int((depth - 2) / 9)
  97:     
  98:         inputs = Input(shape=input_shape)
  99:         # v2 performs Convolution2D with BN-ReLU on input before splitting into 2 paths
 100:         x = resnet_layer(inputs=inputs,
 101:                          num_filters=num_filters_in,
 102:                          kernel_size=11,
 103:                          conv_first=True)
 104:     
 105:         # Instantiate the stack of residual units
 106:         for stage in range(4):
 107:             for res_block in range(num_res_blocks):
 108:                 this_kernal = 3
 109:                 activation = not_quite_linear
 110:                 batch_normalization = False
 111:                 strides = 1
 112:                 if stage == 0:
 113:                     this_kernal = 7
 114:                     num_filters_out = num_filters_in * 2
 115:                     if res_block == 0:  # first layer and first stage
 116:                         activation = None
 117:                         batch_normalization = False
 118:                 else:
 119:                     num_filters_out = num_filters_in * 2
 120:                     if res_block == 0:  # first layer but not first stage
 121:                         strides = 2    # downsample
 122:     
 123:                 # bottleneck residual unit
 124:                 y = resnet_layer(inputs=x,
 125:                                  num_filters=num_filters_in,
 126:                                  kernel_size=3,
 127:                                  strides=strides,
 128:                                  activation=activation,
 129:                                  batch_normalization=batch_normalization,
 130:                                  conv_first=False)
 131: 
 132:                 y = resnet_layer(inputs=y,
 133:                                  num_filters=num_filters_in,
 134:                                  kernel_size=this_kernal,
 135:                                  conv_first=False)
 136:                 y = resnet_layer(inputs=y,
 137:                                  num_filters=num_filters_out,
 138:                                  kernel_size=1,
 139:                                  conv_first=False)
 140:                 if res_block == 0:
 141:                     # linear projection residual shortcut connection to match
 142:                     # changed dims
 143:                     x = resnet_layer(inputs=x,
 144:                                      num_filters=num_filters_out,
 145:                                      kernel_size=3,
 146:                                      strides=strides,
 147:                                      activation=None,
 148:                                      batch_normalization=False)
 149:                 x = keras.layers.add([x, y])
 150:     
 151:             num_filters_in = num_filters_out
 152:     
 153:         # Add classifier on top.
 154:         # v2 has BN-ReLU before Pooling
 155:         x = Activation(not_quite_linear)(x)
 156:         x = AveragePooling2D(pool_size=4)(x)
 157:         y = Flatten()(x)
 158:         outputs = Dense(num_classes,
 159:                         activation=linear_bound_above_abs_1,
 160:                         kernel_initializer='he_normal')(y)
 161:     
 162:         # Instantiate model.
 163:         model = Model(inputs=inputs, outputs=outputs)
 164:         return model
 165: 
 166:     def lr_schedule(epoch):
 167:         """Learning Rate Schedule
 168: 
 169:         Learning rate is scheduled to be reduced after 80, 120, 160, 180 epochs.
 170:         Called automatically every epoch as part of callbacks during training.
 171: 
 172:         # Arguments
 173:             epoch (int): The number of epochs
 174: 
 175:         # Returns
 176:             lr (float32): learning rate
 177:         """
 178:         lr = 1e-4
 179:         if epoch > 180:
 180:             lr *= 0.5e-3
 181:         elif epoch > 160:
 182:             lr *= 1e-3
 183:         elif epoch > 120:
 184:             lr *= 1e-2
 185:         elif epoch > 80:
 186:             lr *= 1e-1
 187:         print('Learning rate: ', lr)
 188:         return lr
